            <div class="asian-voice__main-content">
             <div class="asian-voices__quote">
              <blockquote class="asian-voices__quote-text">
               While Suhartos coup might have ushered in a golden period for the young nation, he knew when to step aside after losing legitimacy.
              </blockquote>
              <p class="asian-voices__quote-author">
               Political scientist Dr Nehginpao Kipgen says Myanmar has missed critical take-aways from Indonesia's democratic transition
              </p>
             </div>

             <div class="asian-voices__quote">
              <blockquote class="asian-voices__quote-text">
               Companies have to reinvent themselves constantly. What makes this case special is that the upstart is reinventing itself at the same time it is close to getting publicly listed.
              </blockquote>
              <p class="asian-voices__quote-author">
               Deliveroo defied fundamentals in 2020 but its prospects do not look good, says IMD Business School Prof Howard Yu
              </p>
